<user>111456217794410863251< /user><Name>Forrest Smith< /Name><Time>1538529377300</Time><Rating>4</Rating>< Text>
Sabre Springs Park is heavily used for both soccer and baseball/softball. There is a small playground for the little ones that is well maintained. There is not much in the way of parking for the size of fields and because of the shear numbers of youth leagues playing nearly year round, the fields have taken quite a beating. The baseball fields are lit for about an hour or so after dark and there is plenty of lighting on the path that leads around the park frequented by runners and walkers. I typically see people using a long set of stairs to workout on located at the entrance of the park and if that isn‚Äôt long enough there is a well worn trail behind the park that will give you plenty of uphill climb. Almost exactly 1/2 mile to the peak. If the fields were in a little better shape I could give this a 5 star rating but it‚Äôs been pretty rough for some time and I haven‚Äôt seen any improvement.< /Text>

Dimitri is outstanding and works hard to meet his customers' needs, while providing humor and care.  He makes it seamless to perform any mailing transaction, and goes the extra mile to help out creatively with other printing issues not necessarily part of standard business.

It is disappointing to read some of the negative reviews.  Sadly, it seems both the anonymity and uncensored freedom of posting, creates an opportunity for some people to deep dive into damaging, poisonous and uncensored diatribes.  This is disheartening both for the harm it can affect on this gentleman's business, and for the corrosion it ultimately causes to our sense of humanity and regard.

Dimitri's Postal Place is a private business. Some people use his business as a post office to drop off their boxes for mailing.  Dimitri provides free mailing to his customers, as a courtesy, with the exception of UPS, which he now charges $1 for most box sizes.  Dimitri's store is not the Post Office, or a UPS store, or a Fedex store.  However, some individuals have the impression his private business is there as a free public service.  It is unfortunate that some of those people who have benefitted from Dimitri's kindnesses and generosity, would so abuse him in this google forum.

I can only suggest to any readers who are investigating postal services for the Santa Monica area, give Dimitri's Postal Place, a fair chance.  There always seems to be room for parking in the back, and items you may need for mailing, readily available, in addition to complete mailing services.

Thank you Dimitri for your service, your care and your integrity.

I set up a 6-month payment plan once I received my bill, everything is fine, right? I set up auto pay and everything. The month before my last payment is due, I get a notice that I had been sent to collections. What the actual f***?

After contacting Cottage, I was informed that my account and some others had been sent by mistake, the collections company should not be contacting me in any way and my credit would not be affected. "Cottage was to reacquire the accounts by the end of the month." I was told to sit and wait, everything was in order to be fixed. *sigh of relief*  Well, I was relieved until three days later (today)...

Today I received a very stern phone call from the collections agency, stating my account was officially assigned to them and was indeed staying in collections.  They reassured me that Cottage informed them on Monday (when I called everyone initially freaking out) that my account is really delinquent... WHAT?! NO!

It was only after I contacted Cottage again, managed a conference call with them (Terri from billing was extremely patient with all this) AND the collections agency (Maria Hernandez), that they were able to cancel the collections on my account. I sure hope everyone else who was accidentally sent to collections didn't have to go through this nonsense. It was a simple fix to a disastrous mistake, luckily. I'm afraid to get too comfortable too soon with this resolution.

But honestly, how easy is it to accidentally send someone to collections? I really want to know. Whoever made this mistake at Cottage should be fired or written up. Attention to detail is critical when you're in charge of customer accounts and billing. People are afraid of hospitals and healthcare enough with inflated prices and insurance troubles. This kind of mess is just icing on the cake.< /review>

< review>
I got the Amazon acai bowl and compared to other acai bowls I've tried this was very disappointing. The size of the item itself leads you to think that it'll be filling, but they add in quite a bit of ice into the acai to essentially make it an acai smoothie.

It's very watery, very little acai flavor. The best part of this was the fruit and granola but that's the best part of ANY acai bowl. On top of that it was $8.

The staff are also not very welcoming and you can tell the owners that work here don't like their jobs.

Only rating this two stars because their boba drinks are good (but I haven't been to a boba place that serves bad beverages, really).< /review>

<Review>Like many establishments, they've setup outdoor dining. Menu is a code to scan on the table. We enjoyed a couple of new items on the menu. The half rack ribs with shrimp and 2 sides and the half rack ribs with chicken. Sauce had a nice flavor, bit too spicy or too sickly sweet. Meat was "fall off the bone" cooked. Coleslaw was crispy fresh, not too vinegary. Also had fries, and that is where plating issues come in. If you put a bunch of fries on the plate and then a rack of hot, juicy, BBQ ribs on top of them, what's going to happen to fries. The ones underneath are soft and soggy. The coleslaw came in a separate small dish which kept it's juice from spreading out underneath the fries as well.
But overall, it was a very good lunchtime break and I would recommend it.</Review>< Pics>

<Rating>2<//Rating>< review>
I use to go to the Coco's in La Mesa all the time, it was wonderful! Unfortunately they closed 2 years ago and I am forced to come here. I usually like them but I had a poor experience on Thanksgiving.

I called to see if they were doing slices of pie because, my mom was in the hospital for the holiday unexpectedly and that was all she wanted and I had already driven around town. Apparently pie is some huge secret because, Katie could not tell me what pies they had. I did the drive all the way down to Coco's from the hospital in Mission Valley only to find out they didn't even make the pie I was looking for. I had told Katie my situation on the phone, I didn't want to make a drive for a pie that didn't exist. She made it seem as if this pie was there. Once I talked to her again and told her what was going on she said, "aww poor baby." very sarcastically, insincere and dismissive. I wanted to cry because, it's just my mom and I living here in San Diego and I'm just a kid trying to manage all of this and give my mom a holiday meal while she's in the hospital.

Once I got into the back area where they were distributing pies (I figured I'd just buy a whole pie, take a slice and give the rest away). They didn't have much left by noon but told me to come back in 4 hours, that's a sick joke. I did talk to a nice woman working and told her my story and she was so sweet about the situation and made recommendations. Miraculously the slice of pie that KATIE told me didn't exist showed up! I appreciated the lady who helped me and another gentleman (guest) for helping me out but I felt that Katie was playing with people's emotions and I didn't appreciate it whatsoever.

Not surprised by Katie's dismissive attitude because, I witnessed her one time saying something explicit to a cook in Spanish. She even admitted it and asked if I spoke Spanish and heard her.</review>
